<script type="text/javascript">
	jQuery(document).ready(function($){
	  $.ajax({
		type 	: "GET",
		dataType: "json",
		url     : "https://www.maltairport.com/wp-content/themes/mia/flightsinfo.php",
		data 	: { arrivalsDepartures_action : "getArrivalsDepartures" },
		success : function(response){
			
			$("#departurestab").html("");
			var departureSectionHTML = 	'<div class="swipe-mobile"></div>' +
										' <table class="arrive-depart-table">' + 
										'<tr><th>Airline</th><th>Flight</th><th>To</th><th>Sch</th><th>Est</th><th>Remarks</th><th>Save Flight</th></tr>';
			
			$.each(response.departures, function(index, value)
			{
				departureSectionHTML 	+= 	'<tr><td><a href="' + value.bookingLink + '" target="_blank">' +
											(value.airlineImage != '' ? '<img src="https://www.maltairport.com' + value.airlineImage + '" />' : value.airlineName) +
											'</a></td>' +
											'<td>' + value.flightNumber + '</td>' +
											'<td>' + value.airportName + '</td>' + 
											'<td>' + value.scheduledTime + '</td>' +
											'<td>' + value.estimatedTime + '</td><td>' +
											(value.remarks != null ? value.remarks : '') +
											'</td>' +
											'<td><img src="https://www.maltairport.com/wp-content/themes/mia/img/icons/bookmark.svg" class="day-icon save-flight" data-flight="' + value.flightNumber + '" alt="" /></td></tr>';
				
			});
			departureSectionHTML 	+= '</table>';
			$("#departurestab").html(departureSectionHTML);
			
			$("#arrivalstab").html("");
			var arrivalsSectionHTML = 	'<div class="swipe-mobile"></div>' +
										' <table class="arrive-depart-table">' + 
										'<tr><th>Airline</th><th>Flight</th><th>From</th><th>Sch</th><th>Est</th><th>Remarks</th><th>Save Flight</th></tr>';
			
			$.each(response.arrivals, function(index, value)
			{
                arrivalsSectionHTML +=	'<tr><td><a href="' + value.bookingLink + '" target="_blank">' +
										(value.airlineImage != '' ? '<img src="https://www.maltairport.com' + value.airlineImage + '" />' : value.airlineName) +
										'</a></td>' +
										'<td>' + value.flightNumber + '</td>' +
										'<td>' + value.airportName + '</td>' + 
										'<td>' + value.scheduledTime + '</td>' +
										'<td>' + value.estimatedTime + '</td><td>' +
										(value.remarks != null ? value.remarks : '') +
										'</td>' +
										'<td><img src="https://www.maltairport.com/wp-content/themes/mia/img/icons/bookmark.svg" class="day-icon save-flight" data-flight="' + value.flightNumber + '" alt="" /></td></tr>';
			});
			arrivalsSectionHTML += '</table>';
			$("#arrivalstab").html(arrivalsSectionHTML);
			
			highlightSavedFlights();
			
		    $('.save-flight').on('click', function () {
				saveFlightClick($(this).data("flight"));
			});
			
			$("#departurestab, #arrivalstab").unblock();
			$("#departurestab .box-inner, #arrivalstab .box-inner").fadeIn();
			
		}
	  });
	});
</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			jQuery(document).ready(function($){
			  $.ajax({
				type 	: "GET",
				dataType: "json",
				url 	: "index.php",
				data 	: { savedFlights_action : "getSavedFlights" },
				success : function(response){
					
					$(".savedFlightsContainer").html("");
					$.each(response.savedFlights, function(index, value)
					{
						$(".savedFlightsContainer").append("<div class='row-bookmark "+ value.isArrival +"'>" +
								"<div class='col-icon'>" + 
									"<img src='https://www.maltairport.com/wp-content/themes/mia/img/icons/flightstatus.svg' alt=''/>"  +
								"</div>" +
								"<div class='col-01'>"+
									"<span class='status'>"+value.remarks+"</span><br>" +
									"<span class='time'>"+value.time+"</span>" +
									"</div><div class='col-02'>" +
									"<span class='details'>"+value.airportName+"</span><br>" +
									"<span class='flightno'>"+value.flightNumber+"</span></div>" +
									"<span class='remove-flight' data-flight='"+value.flightNumber+"'>X</span></div>");
									
					});
					
					if(response.savedFlights.length === 0){
						$(".savedFlightsContainer").append("<div class='description'><img src='https://www.maltairport.com/wp-content/themes/mia/img/icons/bookmark.svg' class='star' alt=''/><span class='text'>"+ response.savedFlightsDesc +"</span></div>");
					}
					
					$("#saved-flights.info-box").unblock();
					$("#saved-flights.info-box .box-inner").fadeIn();
					
					$('.remove-flight').on('click', function () {
						removeFlightClick($(this).data("flight"));
					});
					
				}
			  });
			});
		</script>
